Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageWellTower partner Balfour Senior Living contact form
URLhttps://www.balfourcare.com/company/contact
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro
Test date2023/04/23
Score1138
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1138, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 290. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

solos: Score 10. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue menuNavigation

WCAG: 2.1.1

Score: 112

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test menuNav, score 110 (Nonstandard keyboard navigation among focusable menu items)

Issue overflowHidden

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 106

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r83, score 92 (Overflow is hidden or clipped if the text is enlarged)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R40, score 30 (Zoomed text node is clipped by a CSS overflow declaration)

Issue linkNoText

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 68

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r11, score 20 (Link has no accessible name)
  • Package axe, test link-name, score 15 (Link has no discernible text)
  • Package continuum, test 237, score 20 (a element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name value to be calculated)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_2.H91.A.NoContent, score 20 (Link has an href attribute but no text)
  • Package ibm, test WCAG20_A_HasText, score 20 (Hyperlink has no text description)
  • Package wave, test e:link_empty, score 20 (Link contains no text)
  • Package tenon, test 57, score 20 (Link has no text inside it)

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 62

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 1 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 60 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue tabFocusability

WCAG: 2.1.1

Score: 56

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focAll, score 54 (Discrepancy between elements that should be and that are Tab-focusable)

Issue svgImageNoText

WCAG: 1.1.1

Score: 50

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package continuum, test 123, score 48 (svg element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name to be calculated)

Score: 47
